\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addUsesDependency()}{addUsesDependency()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Dir\+Def\+Impl\+::add\+Uses\+Dependency (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_dir_def}{Dir\+Def}} $\ast$}]{dir,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_file_def}{File\+Def}} $\ast$}]{src\+Fd,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_file_def}{File\+Def}} $\ast$}]{dst\+Fd,  }\item[{bool}]{src\+Direct,  }\item[{bool}]{dst\+Direct }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Add as \char`\"{}uses\char`\"{} dependency between {\itshape this} dir and {\itshape dir}, that was caused by a dependency on file {\itshape fd}. src\+Direct and dst\+Direct indicate if it is a direct dependencies (true) or if the dependencies was indirect (e.\+g. a parent dir that has a child dir that has the dependencies) 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{class_dir_def_a7080956a2fe6049dc2fa115cfd1aef5b}{Dir\+Def}}.
